```
â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

PROMPT 6: SYSTEM_PROMPT_REPORT_FORMATTING
â”œâ”€ Ğ’Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´:
â”‚  â””â”€ report_data: [
â”‚       {
â”‚         title: paragraphs[0].title,
â”‚         paragraph_latest_state: paragraphs[0].research.latest_summary
â”‚       },
â”‚       ... (5 Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€Ğ°Ñ„Ğ¾Ğ², ĞºĞ°Ğ¶Ğ´Ñ‹Ğ¹ 1000-1500 ÑĞ»Ğ¾Ğ²)
â”‚     ]
â”‚     Ğ˜Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾: ~5000-7500 ÑĞ»Ğ¾Ğ² Ğ²Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ… Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ…
â”‚
â”œâ”€ Ğ—Ğ°Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‡Ğ°:
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ¾Ñ‚Ñ‡ĞµÑ‚ 10 000+ ÑĞ»Ğ¾Ğ²
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Ğ”Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Executive Summary
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ Ñ‚Ğ°Ğ±Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ†Ñ‹ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ…
â”‚  â”œâ”€ Ğ”Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ ÑĞ¼Ğ¾Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½ÑƒÑ Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ·ÑƒĞ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ
â”‚  â”œâ”€ ĞĞ°Ğ¿Ğ¸ÑĞ°Ñ‚ÑŒ comprehensive analysis (ĞºĞ¾Ğ¼Ğ¿Ğ»ĞµĞºÑĞ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ°Ğ½Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ·)
```

### 1.3 ĞšĞ¾Ğ½Ñ„Ğ¸Ğ³ÑƒÑ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ°Ğ¼ĞµÑ‚Ñ€Ñ‹

## 2. QueryEngine - ĞŸĞ°Ğ¹Ğ¿Ğ»Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ½ Ğ°Ğ½Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ° Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ĞµĞ¹

## 3. MediaEngine - ĞŸĞ°Ğ¹Ğ¿Ğ»Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ½ Ğ¼ÑƒĞ»ÑŒÑ‚Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾ Ğ°Ğ½Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°

**ĞĞ°Ğ·Ğ½Ğ°Ñ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ:** ĞœÑƒĞ»ÑŒÑ‚Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ°Ğ½Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ· ĞºĞ¾Ğ½Ñ‚ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ°, Ğ¸Ğ½Ñ‚ĞµĞ³Ñ€Ğ¸Ñ€ÑƒÑÑ‰Ğ¸Ğ¹ Ñ‚ĞµĞºÑÑ‚, Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ğ¶ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ, AI-Ñ€ĞµĞ·ÑĞ¼Ğµ Ğ¸ ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ.

### 3.1 ĞĞ±Ñ‰Ğ°Ñ ÑÑ…ĞµĞ¼Ğ° Ğ¿Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ¿Ğ»Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ½Ğ°

```
  â†“

  â†“

```

### 3.2 Ğ˜Ğ½ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ñ‹ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ¸ÑĞºĞ° MediaEngine


### 4.3 ĞœĞµÑ…Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¼ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ¸ Ğ³Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ½Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¸ Ğ²Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ… Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ²

### 4.4 ĞšĞ¾Ğ½Ñ„Ğ¸Ğ³ÑƒÑ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ°Ğ¼ĞµÑ‚Ñ€Ñ‹

## 5. ForumEngine - ĞŸĞ°Ğ¹Ğ¿Ğ»Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ½ Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ´ĞµÑ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ¼ÑƒĞ»ÑŒÑ‚Ğ¸Ğ°Ğ³ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ… Ğ´Ğ¸ÑĞºÑƒÑÑĞ¸Ğ¹

**ĞĞ°Ğ·Ğ½Ğ°Ñ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ:** Ğ ĞµĞ°Ğ»-Ñ‚Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ¼ Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ³ Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾Ğ² Ñ‚Ñ€ĞµÑ… Ğ°Ğ½Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑĞºĞ¸Ñ… Ğ´Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ¶ĞºĞ¾Ğ², Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ²Ğ»ĞµÑ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ¸Ñ… "Ğ²Ñ‹ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¹" Ğ¸ Ğ³ĞµĞ½ĞµÑ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ´ĞµÑ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ¾Ñ‚ AI-Ñ…Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ°.

**Ğ˜ÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ‡Ğ½Ğ¸Ğº Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ…:** 
- logs/insight.log
- logs/media.log
- logs/query.log

**Ğ¤Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»Ñ‹:** 
- `ForumEngine/monitor.py` - LogMonitor (Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ³ Ğ¸ Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ²Ğ»ĞµÑ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ)
- `ForumEngine/llm_host.py` - AI Host (Ğ³ĞµĞ½ĞµÑ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ´ĞµÑ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸)

### 5.1 ĞĞ±Ñ‰Ğ°Ñ ÑÑ…ĞµĞ¼Ğ° Ğ¿Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ¿Ğ»Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ½Ğ°

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”

â”‚ â”‚ You are a forum moderator for a multi-agent public opinion    â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚ analysis system. Your responsibilities are:                    â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚                                                                 â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚ 1. Event Organization: Identify key events, people, time nodesâ”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚    from each agent's statements, organize timeline            â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚ 2. Guide Discussion: Based on statements, guide in-depth      â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚    discussion, explore underlying causes                       â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚ 3. Correct Errors: If factual errors or logical contradictionsâ”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚    found, clearly point them out                               â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚ 4. Integrate Perspectives: Synthesize different viewpoints,   â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚    form comprehensive understanding                            â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚ 5. Trend Prediction: Analyze trends, propose risk points      â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚ 6. Advance Analysis: Propose new analytical perspectives      â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚                                                                 â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚ Agent Introductions:                                           â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚   - INSIGHT: Focuses on private opinion DB, historical patternsâ”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚   - MEDIA: Excels at multimodal content, visual communication â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚   - QUERY: Responsible for precise searches, real-time info   â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚                                                                 â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚ Speaking Requirements:                                         â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚   - Comprehensiveness: Control within 1000 words              â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚   - Clear Structure: Event org, perspective comparison, Q&A   â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚   - In-depth Analysis: Propose deep insights                  â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚   - Objective Neutrality: Analyze based on facts              â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚   - Forward-looking: Propose forward-looking suggestions      â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚                                                                 â”‚   â”‚

â”‚ â”‚ As the forum moderator, please conduct comprehensive analysis â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚ according to the following structure:                          â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚                                                                 â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚ I. Event Organization and Timeline Analysis                   â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚    - Identify key events, people, time nodes                  â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚    - Organize timeline, clarify causal relationships          â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚    - Point out key turning points                             â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚                                                                 â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚ II. Perspective Integration and Comparative Analysis          â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚    - Synthesize perspectives from INSIGHT, MEDIA, QUERY       â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚    - Point out consensus and divergences                      â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚    - Analyze information value and complementarity            â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚    - If errors or contradictions found, point out with reasonsâ”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚                                                                 â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚ III. Deep-level Analysis and Trend Prediction                 â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚    - Analyze deep causes and influencing factors              â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚    - Predict trends, point out risk points and opportunities  â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚    - Propose aspects requiring special attention              â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚                                                                 â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚ IV. Question Guidance and Discussion Direction                â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚    - Propose 2-3 key questions for further exploration        â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚    - Provide specific suggestions for subsequent research     â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚    - Guide agents to focus on specific data dimensions        â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚                                                                 â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚ Please deliver comprehensive moderator statement (within 1000 â”‚   â”‚
â”‚ â”‚ words), including the above four parts with clear logic.      â”‚   â”‚

â”‚ ĞŸĞ¾ÑĞ»Ğµ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ²ĞµÑ€ÑˆĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ:                                                    â”‚
â”‚   - Ğ’Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ²Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‚ Ğ² Ğ¤ĞĞ—Ğ£ 1 (Ğ¾Ğ¶Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾ Ñ‚Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ³Ğ³ĞµÑ€Ğ°)                    â”‚
â”‚   - Ğ¡Ğ±Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ Ğ²ÑĞµÑ… ÑĞ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ÑĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¹:                                           â”‚
â”‚     â€¢ agent_speeches_buffer = []                                    â”‚
â”‚     â€¢ is_host_generating = False                                    â”‚
â”‚     â€¢ capturing_json = {}                                           â”‚
â”‚     â€¢ json_buffer = {}                                              â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
  â”‚
  â–¼
OUTPUT: logs/forum.log (Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ¶ÑƒÑ€Ğ½Ğ°Ğ» Ğ´Ğ¸ÑĞºÑƒÑÑĞ¸Ğ¹)
```


### 5.3 Key Technical Details

#### 5.3.1 ERROR Block Filtering (ĞºÑ€Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑĞºĞ¸ Ğ²Ğ°Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ¾!)

```python
# ForumEngine/monitor.py

# ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ»ĞµĞ¼Ğ°: Ğ’ Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ°Ñ… Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ³ÑƒÑ‚ Ğ±Ñ‹Ñ‚ÑŒ ERROR ÑƒÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ½Ğ¸ Ñ JSON-Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¼ ĞºĞ¾Ğ½Ñ‚ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ¼,
#           ĞºĞ¾Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ñ‹Ğµ ĞĞ• ÑĞ²Ğ»ÑÑÑ‚ÑÑ Ñ€ĞµĞ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğ¼Ğ¸ Ğ²Ñ‹ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸ÑĞ¼Ğ¸ Ğ°Ğ³ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²

# Ğ ĞµÑˆĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ: ĞÑ‚ÑĞ»ĞµĞ¶Ğ¸Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ ERROR/INFO ÑĞ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ÑĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¹

def process_lines_for_json(lines, app_name):
    for line in lines:
        log_level = get_log_level(line)  # Ğ˜Ğ·Ğ²Ğ»ĞµÑ‡ÑŒ: INFO, ERROR, WARNING, ...
        
        if log_level == 'ERROR':
            # Ğ’Ğ¾Ğ¹Ñ‚Ğ¸ Ğ² ERROR block
            in_error_block[app_name] = True
            # Ğ•ÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ·Ğ°Ñ…Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚Ñ‹Ğ²Ğ°Ğ»ÑÑ JSON, Ğ½ĞµĞ¼ĞµĞ´Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ½Ğ¾ Ğ¿Ñ€ĞµÑ€Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ
            if capturing_json[app_name]:
                capturing_json[app_name] = False
                json_buffer[app_name] = []
            continue  # ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ¿ÑƒÑÑ‚Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ²ÑÑ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¾ĞºÑƒ
        
        elif log_level == 'INFO':
            # Ğ’Ñ‹Ğ¹Ñ‚Ğ¸ Ğ¸Ğ· ERROR block
            in_error_block[app_name] = False
        
        # Ğ•ÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ² ERROR block, Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ¿ÑƒÑÑ‚Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ’Ğ¡Ğ
        if in_error_block[app_name]:
            continue
        
        # ĞĞ±Ñ‹Ñ‡Ğ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ‚ĞºĞ° (Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞºĞ¾ ĞµÑĞ»Ğ¸ ĞĞ• Ğ² ERROR block)
        ...
```

#### 5.3.2 ĞœĞ½Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ‡Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ JSON Capture

```python
# ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ»ĞµĞ¼Ğ°: LLM Ğ²Ñ‹Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´ Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ¶ĞµÑ‚ Ğ±Ñ‹Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¼Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ‡Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¼:
#   [10:30:15] [InsightEngine] Cleaned output: {
#   [10:30:15]   "paragraph_latest_state": "## Core Findings\n\nWuhan University..."
#   [10:30:15] }

# Ğ ĞµÑˆĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ: State Machine Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ·Ğ°Ñ…Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ°

capturing_json[app_name] = False  # ĞĞµ Ğ·Ğ°Ñ…Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚Ñ‹Ğ²Ğ°ĞµÑ‚ÑÑ
json_buffer[app_name] = []        # Ğ‘ÑƒÑ„ĞµÑ€ Ğ¿ÑƒÑÑ‚

# ĞšĞ¾Ğ³Ğ´Ğ° Ğ²ÑÑ‚Ñ€ĞµÑ‡Ğ°ĞµÑ‚ÑÑ "Cleaned output: {"
if is_json_start_line(line):
    capturing_json[app_name] = True
    json_buffer[app_name] = [line]
    
    # ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ: ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ single-line JSON?
    if line.strip().endswith("}"):
        content = extract_json_content([line])
        write_to_forum_log(content, app_name.upper())
        capturing_json[app_name] = False
        json_buffer[app_name] = []

# ĞŸĞ¾ÑĞ»ĞµĞ´ÑƒÑÑ‰Ğ¸Ğµ ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¾ĞºĞ¸
elif capturing_json[app_name]:
    json_buffer[app_name].append(line)
    
    # ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ ĞºĞ¾Ğ½ĞµÑ† (Ğ¿Ğ¾ÑĞ»Ğµ Ğ¾Ñ‡Ğ¸ÑÑ‚ĞºĞ¸ timestamp)
    cleaned_line = remove_timestamp(line).strip()
    if cleaned_line == "}" or cleaned_line == "] }":
        # ĞšĞ¾Ğ½ĞµÑ† JSON, Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ
        content = extract_json_content(json_buffer[app_name])
        write_to_forum_log(content, app_name.upper())
        capturing_json[app_name] = False
        json_buffer[app_name] = []
```

#### 5.3.3 Thread Safety

```python
# ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ»ĞµĞ¼Ğ°: ĞĞµÑĞºĞ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞºĞ¾ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¾ĞºĞ¾Ğ² Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ³ÑƒÑ‚ Ğ¿Ğ¸ÑĞ°Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ² forum.log Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ñ€ĞµĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ğ½Ğ¾
#   - Ğ¤Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğº Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ³Ğ°
#   - Ğ¡Ğ¸Ğ½Ñ…Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ² HOST Ğ³ĞµĞ½ĞµÑ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸

# Ğ ĞµÑˆĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ: Threading Lock

write_lock = Lock()

def write_to_forum_log(content, source):
    with write_lock:  # Ğ­ĞºÑĞºĞ»ÑĞ·Ğ¸Ğ²Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ´Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿
        with open(forum_log_file, 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            timestamp = datetime.now().strftime('%H:%M:%S')
            # ĞšĞ¾Ğ½Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ \n Ğ² \\n Ğ´Ğ»Ñ single-line Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ğ¸ÑĞ¸
            content_one_line = content.replace('\n', '\\n')
            f.write(f"[{timestamp}] [{source}] {content_one_line}\n")
            f.flush()
```

### 5.4 ĞšĞ¾Ğ½Ñ„Ğ¸Ğ³ÑƒÑ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ°Ğ¼ĞµÑ‚Ñ€Ñ‹

```python
# ForumEngine ĞºĞ¾Ğ½Ñ„Ğ¸Ğ³ÑƒÑ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ

# LLM Ğ´Ğ»Ñ HOST Ğ¼Ğ¾Ğ´ĞµÑ€Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ°
FORUM_ENGINE_API_KEY: str
FORUM_ENGINE_MODEL_NAME: str
FORUM_ENGINE_BASE_URL: str

# Ğ”Ğ¸Ñ€ĞµĞºÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾Ğ²
LOG_DIR: str = "logs"
MONITORED_LOGS: Dict[str, str] = {
    'insight': 'logs/insight.log',
    'media': 'logs/media.log',
    'query': 'logs/query.log'
}
FORUM_LOG_FILE: str = "logs/forum.log"

# ĞŸĞ¾Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¸
HOST_SPEECH_THRESHOLD: int = 5   # ĞšĞ°Ğ¶Ğ´Ñ‹Ğµ 5 Ğ²Ñ‹ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¹ â†’ HOST
SEARCH_INACTIVE_TIMEOUT: int = 7200  # 2 Ñ‡Ğ°ÑĞ° Ğ±ĞµĞ· Ğ°ĞºÑ‚Ğ¸Ğ²Ğ½Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¸
MONITOR_INTERVAL: int = 1  # ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ° ĞºĞ°Ğ¶Ğ´ÑƒÑ 1 ÑĞµĞºÑƒĞ½Ğ´Ñƒ
```

## 6. MindSpider - ĞŸĞ°Ğ¹Ğ¿Ğ»Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ½ ÑĞ±Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ° Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ…

**ĞĞ°Ğ·Ğ½Ğ°Ñ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ:** ĞĞ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑĞºĞ¸Ğ¹ ÑĞ±Ğ¾Ñ€ ĞºĞ¾Ğ½Ñ‚ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ° Ğ¸Ğ· ĞºĞ¸Ñ‚Ğ°Ğ¹ÑĞºĞ¸Ñ… ÑĞ¾Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ñ… Ğ¼ĞµĞ´Ğ¸Ğ° Ğ¿Ğ»Ğ°Ñ‚Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼ Ğ¸ ÑĞ¾Ñ…Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ² Ğ»Ğ¾ĞºĞ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½ÑƒÑ Ğ±Ğ°Ğ·Ñƒ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ… PostgreSQL Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ğ¾ÑĞ»ĞµĞ´ÑƒÑÑ‰ĞµĞ³Ğ¾ Ğ°Ğ½Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ° InsightEngine.

**Ğ˜ÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ‡Ğ½Ğ¸Ğº Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ…:** 7 ĞºĞ¸Ñ‚Ğ°Ğ¹ÑĞºĞ¸Ñ… ÑĞ¾Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ñ… Ğ¼ĞµĞ´Ğ¸Ğ° Ğ¿Ğ»Ğ°Ñ‚Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼ Ñ‡ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ· MediaCrawler Ñ„Ñ€ĞµĞ¹Ğ¼Ğ²Ğ¾Ñ€Ğº

**Ğ¤Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»:** `MindSpider/main.py`


### 6.2 ĞÑ€Ñ…Ğ¸Ñ‚ĞµĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ğ° Ğ±Ğ°Ğ·Ñ‹ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ…

```sql
-- MindSpider/schema/models_bigdata.py â†’ SQL

-- â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
-- Ğ¢ĞĞ‘Ğ›Ğ˜Ğ¦Ğ« ĞšĞ›Ğ®Ğ§Ğ•Ğ’Ğ«Ğ¥ Ğ¡Ğ›ĞĞ’
-- â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

CREATE TABLE daily_topics (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    date DATE NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    summary TEXT,                     -- Ğ ĞµĞ·ÑĞ¼Ğµ Ğ´Ğ½Ñ Ğ¾Ñ‚ LLM
    keyword_count INTEGER,            -- ĞšĞ¾Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²Ğ¾ ĞºĞ»ÑÑ‡ĞµĞ²Ñ‹Ñ… ÑĞ»Ğ¾Ğ²
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE TABLE extracted_keywords (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    keyword VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    weight FLOAT DEFAULT 1.0,         -- Ğ’ĞµÑ ĞºĞ»ÑÑ‡ĞµĞ²Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾ ÑĞ»Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ° (0-1)
    source VARCHAR(50),               -- Ğ˜ÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ‡Ğ½Ğ¸Ğº (baidu/weibo/...)
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    UNIQUE(date, keyword)
);

-- â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
-- Ğ¢ĞĞ‘Ğ›Ğ˜Ğ¦Ğ« ĞšĞĞĞ¢Ğ•ĞĞ¢Ğ (Ğ´Ğ»Ñ ĞºĞ°Ğ¶Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ¹ Ğ¿Ğ»Ğ°Ñ‚Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ñ‹)
-- â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

-- 1. Bilibili
CREATE TABLE bilibili_posts (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    platform_id VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE,   -- BVå·
    keyword VARCHAR(100),
    title_or_content TEXT,
    author_nickname VARCHAR(100),
    publish_time TIMESTAMP,
    url TEXT,
    hotness_score BIGINT,
    engagement JSONB,                 -- {likes, comments, shares, views}
    content_type VARCHAR(20),         -- 'post' or 'comment'
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE TABLE bilibili_comments (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    post_id INTEGER REFERENCES bilibili_posts(id),
    platform_comment_id VARCHAR(50),
    content TEXT,
    author_nickname VARCHAR(100),
    publish_time TIMESTAMP,
    like_count INTEGER,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- 2. Weibo
CREATE TABLE weibo_posts (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    platform_id VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE,
    keyword VARCHAR(100),
    title_or_content TEXT,
    author_nickname VARCHAR(100),
    publish_time TIMESTAMP,
    url TEXT,
    hotness_score BIGINT,
    engagement JSONB,
    images JSONB,                     -- ĞœĞ°ÑÑĞ¸Ğ² URL Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ğ¶ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğ¹
    content_type VARCHAR(20),
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE TABLE weibo_comments (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    post_id INTEGER REFERENCES weibo_posts(id),
    platform_comment_id VARCHAR(50),
    content TEXT,
    author_nickname VARCHAR(100),
    publish_time TIMESTAMP,
    like_count INTEGER,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- 3-7. ĞĞ½Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¸Ñ‡Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ñ‚Ğ°Ğ±Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ†Ñ‹ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Douyin, Kuaishou, Xiaohongshu, Zhihu, Tieba
-- ... (ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ğ° Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ¶Ğ°Ñ, Ñ Ğ½ĞµĞ±Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒÑˆĞ¸Ğ¼Ğ¸ Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸ÑĞ¼Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ĞµĞ¹)
```

### 6.3 ĞšĞ¾Ğ½Ñ„Ğ¸Ğ³ÑƒÑ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ°Ğ¼ĞµÑ‚Ñ€Ñ‹

```python

# PostgreSQL ĞºĞ¾Ğ½Ñ„Ğ¸Ğ³ÑƒÑ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ

# MediaCrawler ĞºĞ¾Ğ½Ñ„Ğ¸Ğ³ÑƒÑ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ

    "bilibili", "weibo", "douyin", 
    "kuaishou", "xiaohongshu", "zhihu", "tieba"
]

# Ğ Ğ°ÑĞ¿Ğ¸ÑĞ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ (Ğ¾Ğ¿Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾)
```
